Last Modified   : 2026-02-18 14:58:08
SHA-256         : d3378e71576ceb23f7779a571f32b4658148da9328f6c6d8da84a709e0c86a87

Explanation:
Adversaries may encrypt data on target systems or on large numbers of systems in a network to interrupt availability to system and network resources. They can attempt to render stored data inaccessible by encrypting files or data on local and remote drives and withholding access to a decryption key.

Mitigation Steps
----------------
Step 1: Immediately isolate the system from the network.
Step 2: Do NOT execute the file.
Step 3: Perform a full malware scan using updated antivirus.
Step 4: Check for mass file modification or encryption.
Step 5: Restore data from verified backups.
Step 6: Report the incident to cybersecurity team.
